let RTM_Submitter_record_FIRST_0001( RTM_p0 ) = {
Let Total_Hire_Exempt_Wages = 0
Let Total_Roth457 = 0
Let Total_UETT = 0
Let File_ID = RTM_p0
Let TEC = ""
Let city_name = ""
Let city_length = ""

Let Total_409A = 0 
}
let RTM_SRC_Submitter_record_0002(  ) = {
RETURN "1393"
}
let RTM_SRC_Submitter_record_0003(  ) = {

let RTM_Employer_Record_EACH_0006( RTM_p0, RTM_p1 ) = {
Let ER_Code = left(RTM_p0,1)
Let ER_Type = right(RTM_p1,1)

}
let RTM_Employee_Record_EACH_0007( RTM_p0, RTM_p1, RTM_p2, RTM_p3, RTM_p4, RTM_p5, RTM_p6, RTM_p7, RTM_p8, RTM_p9, RTM_p10, RTM_p11, RTM_p12, RTM_p13, RTM_p14, RTM_p15, RTM_p16, RTM_p17 ) = {
If left(RTM_p0,1) = "9" then
 Let SSNSPAD = "000000000"
else
Let SSNSPAD= RTM_p1
endif


let FN=RTM_p2
let MN=RTM_p3
let LN=RTM_p4
let Suffixspad=RTM_p5
let Laddress=RTM_p6
let DAddress=RTM_p7
let C=RTM_p8
let state=RTM_p9
let zip=RTM_p10
let FSP=RTM_p11
let FPC=RTM_p12
Let CC = RTM_p13
If RTM_p14 < "0.00" then
Let DCB = RTM_p15 * "-1"
else
Let DCB = RTM_p16
endif
Let Total_409A = Total_409A + RTM_p17
}
let RTM_SRC_Employee_Record_0008(  ) = {
RETURN SSNSPAD
}
let RTM_SRC_Employee_Record_0009( RTM_p0 ) = {
RETURN LEFT(RTM_p0,1)
}
let RTM_SRC_Employee_Record_0010(  ) = {
RETURN DCB
}
let RTM_Employee_Wage_Record_EACH_0011( RTM_p0, RTM_p1, RTM_p2, RTM_p3 ) = {
If RTM_p0 < "0.00" then
Let UETT = RTM_p1 * "-1"
else
Let UETT = RTM_p2
endif

Let Total_UETT = Total_UETT + UETT
Let Total_Roth457 = Total_Roth457 + RTM_p3
}
let RTM_SRC_Employee_Wage_Record_0012(  ) = {
RETURN UETT
}
let RTM_State_Record_EACH_0013( RTM_p0, RTM_p1, RTM_p2, RTM_p3, RTM_p4, RTM_p5 ) = {
If File_ID = "RITAW2" then
 Let TEC = "RO"++left(RTM_p0,3)
else
If File_ID = "LAPEW2" then
 Let TEC = "LAP"
else
If File_ID = "TIFFW2" then
 Let TEC = "KETTE"
else
If File_ID = "RAVEW2" then
 Let TEC = ""
else
If File_ID = "FINDW2" then
 Let TEC = "FINDL"
else
 Let TEC = RTM_p1
endif
endif
endif
endif
endif

Let city_length = size(RTM_p2)


If File_ID = "RITAW2" then
 Let city_name = RIGHT(RTM_p3,city_length-3)
else
 Let city_name = RTM_p4
endif

If File_ID = "GRRPW2" then
 Let OSD = "GRAND RAP "
else
 Let OSD = RTM_p5
endif

}
let RTM_SRC_State_Record_0014(  ) = {
RETURN TEC
}
let RTM_SRC_State_Record_0015(  ) = {
RETURN LEFT(MN,1)
}
let RTM_SRC_State_Record_0016(  ) = {
RETURN OSD
}
let RTM_SRC_State_Record_0017(  ) = {
RETURN city_name
}
let RTM_Total_Record_EACH_0018( RTM_p0, RTM_p1, RTM_p2 ) = {
If RTM_p0 < "0.00" then
Let DCB_Total = RTM_p1 * "-1"
else
Let DCB_Total = RTM_p2
endif
}
let RTM_SRC_Total_Record_0019(  ) = {
RETURN DCB_Total
}

;
; Driver code: for alpha this will manually
; load the data file and the map definition.
; Eventually this will be replaced with the
; AppScan inbound/outbound queue support.
;
; (AppScan will also provide the name of the batch file

; with deriving a name from the map-def: 'outbound\efw2-ssa.dat'.)
;
;----------------------------------------

IF RTM_RESULT <> 1 THEN
   ECHO "Unable to test map."
   END 1
ENDIF
ECHO "Macro EFW2 completed."
END 0
